
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 Destroy peroxysome biosynthesizing factor protein (PEX) to change polyunsaturated fatty acid and total lipid content in oleaginous eukaryotic organisms 
 The right of priority of patent application claims U.S. Provisional Application 60/977,174 and 60/977,177, described provisional application is all filed on October 3rd, 2007, and incorporated herein by reference in full. 
 
 Invention field 
 The invention belongs to biological technical field.More particularly, the present invention relates to based on destroy the peroxysome biosynthesizing factor (PEX) albumen, for handling the method for Eukaryotic polyunsaturated fatty acid (PUFA) composition and lipid content. 
 
 
 
 background of invention 
 
 Lot of documents has been had to demonstrate and polyunsaturated fatty acid [" PUFA "], the healthy and helpful effect that especially ω-3 is relevant with ω-6PUFA.ω-3 and ω-6 is prepared on a large scale in order to find 
 The method of PUFA, their work has been turned to the biosynthetic pathway finding gene and understand the coding producing lipid and lipid acid by investigator. 
 ω-3/ ω-6PUFA biosynthetic pathway has imported by achievement in research for the production of these PUFA can not in the organism of natural generation ω-3/ ω-6PUFA.The described biology be widely used is a non-saccharomyces olei, Saccharomyces cerevisiae (Saccharomycescerevisiae).But, there is no the linolic acid [" LA "] of PRELIMINARY RESULTS proof limited production, gamma-linolenic acid [" GLA "], alpha-linolenic acid [" ALA "], therapic acid [" STA "] and/or timnodonic acid [" EPA "] and be suitable for business development. 
 Other achievement in research for scale operation ω-3/ ω-6PUFA has cultivated the microorganism that lipid acid is selected in natural production, the filamentous fungus of such as heterotrophic diatoms Cyclotella (Cyclotellasp.) and Nitzschia (Nitzschiasp.), Rhodopseudomonas (Pseudomonas), Alteromonas (Alteromonas) or Shewanella (Shewanella), pythium (Pythium) or long genus mortierella (Mortierellaelongata), M.exigua or M.hygrophila. 
 But all these achievements in research all can not improve the characteristic of the oil composition that oil yield or control are produced fully, because fermentation relies on the native abilities of microorganism itself. 
 Total United States Patent (USP) 7,238,482 describes and uses saccharomyces olei Yarrowia lipolytica as producing the purposes of host for the production of PUFA.Saccharomyces olei be defined as be those natural can synthesize and gather oil yeast, wherein dry cell weight is generally greater than 25%.This area has described the optimization (see such as international application open WO2006/033723, U.S. Patent Application Publication 2006-0094092, U.S. Patent Application Publication 2006-0115881 and U.S. Patent Application Publication 2006-0110806) of producing host.Recombinant bacterial strain as herein described comprises multiple mosaic gene, the allos desaturase of described genetic expression multiple copied, extends enzyme and acyltransferase, and optionally comprises multiple natural desaturase and acyltransferase knocks out can synthesize and gather PUFA.Commercial production PUFA needs to optimize further host cell. 
 LinY. people is waited to propose katabolism that peroxysome is lipid and anabolism necessary (PlantPhysiology, 135:814-827 (2004)).But, this hypothesis is based on the research to the Pex16p homologue in Arabidopsis mutants, this mutant has abnormal peroxysome biosynthesizing and lipid acid synthesis (that is, it is reported that the oil ratio wild-type of producing in ssel seed decreases about 10-16%).The people such as Binns, D. (J.CellBiol., 173 (5): 719-731 (2006)) also provide the document proving peroxysome and the close collaboration of liposome in Saccharomyces cerevisiae.But in the biology producing PUFA, not yet carried out the research that Pex is knocked out in the past. 
 Applicant by destroying the non-precognition mechanism of peroxysome biosynthesizing factor protein in the organism producing PUFA, solve and optimize the described problem of host cell for PUFA commercial production, described mechanism causes producing at the restructuring PUFA of Yarrowia lipolytica the unforeseen outcome improving PUFA amount (representing with total fatty acids percents) in bacterial strain.This document describes the novel strain that there is destruction in peroxysome biosynthesizing factor protein. 
 
 
 
 summary of the invention 
 
 As herein described be improve in the oleaginous eukaryotic organisms with total lipid content, total lipid fraction and oily fraction at least one polyunsaturated fatty acid [" PUFA "] % by weight relative to total fatty acids [" TFA "] % by weight method, described method comprises: 
 A) provide oleaginous eukaryotic organisms, described oleaginous eukaryotic organisms comprises: 
 1) gene of encode functional polyunsaturated fatty acid biosynthetic pathway; With 
 2) destruction in the natural gene of coding peroxidase body biosynthesizing factor protein, provides the biology that PEX destroys thus, and 
 B) biology described PEX being destroyed grows under the following conditions: namely, make when comparing relative to the weight percent of at least one polyunsaturated fatty acid of the weight percent of total fatty acids in the total lipid fraction in the oleaginous eukaryotic organisms that the natural gene with coding peroxidase body biosynthesizing factor protein is not destroyed or oily fraction, in described total lipid fraction or oily fraction, the weight percent of at least one polyunsaturated fatty acid improves relative to the weight percent of total fatty acids. 
 This raising method also by implementing same steps (a) and (b), for improving the per-cent of at least one polyunsaturated fatty acid [" PUFA "] relative to dry cell wt [" DCW "]. 
 In certain methods as herein described, PUFA % by weight improves at least 1.3 times relative to TFA % by weight. 
 In methods described in some, the total lipid content in the organism that PEX destroys may improve with natural PEX gene or reduce compared with the total lipid content of the oleaginous eukaryotic organisms destroyed. 
 In any one of these methods, the PUFA of raising can be the combination of single PUFA or multiple PUFA.In any one situation, the PUFA combination of the PUFA of raising or raising can comprise linolic acid, conjugated linolic acid, gamma-linolenic acid, dihomo-gamma-linolenic acid, arachidonic acid, docosatetratenoic acid, ω-6 clupanodonic acid, alpha-linolenic acid, therapic acid, eicosatetraenoic acid, timnodonic acid, ω-3 clupanodonic acid, eicosadienoic acid, eicosatrienoic acid, docosahexenoic acid, the hydroxylation of these lipid acid or epoxyfatty acid, C

 detailed Description Of The Invention 
 
 As herein described be for handle produce PUFA eukaryote in the concentration (representing with total fatty acids percents) of long chain polyunsaturated fatty acids [" LC-PUFA "] and the universal method of content (representing with dry cell wt percents).These methods depend on to be destroyed the natural peroxide enzyme body biosynthesizing factor [" Pex "] albumen in host and has broad applicability by the multiple eukaryote of the PUFA throughput with natural or genetic engineering, and described eukaryote comprises algae, fungi, oomycetes, yeast, class eye worm, stramenopiles, plant and some mammlian systems. 
 PUFA or derivatives thereof can be used as dietary substitute or supplement, especially infant formula (formula), for accepting the patient of intravenous alimentation or being used for preventing or treatment malnutrition.Such as, PUFA can mix culinary art oil, fat or oleomargarine and general diet part as human consumer is ingested, thus gives the dietary supplement needed for human consumer.In addition, PUFA can also mix in infant formula, nutritious supplementary or other food, and can be used as anti-inflammatory or cholesterol-lowering agent.Optionally, said composition may be used for medicinal (people's medicine or veterinary drug). 
 
 definition 
 
 In the disclosure, a large amount of term and abbreviation is employed.Give as given a definition. 
 " open reading frame " is abbreviated as ORF. 
 " polymerase chain reaction " is abbreviated as PCR. 
 " American type culture collection " is abbreviated as " ATCC ". 
 " polyunsaturated fatty acid " is abbreviated as " PUFA ". 
 " triacylglycerol " is abbreviated as " TAG ". 
 " total fatty acids " is abbreviated as " TFA ". 
 " fatty acid methyl ester " is abbreviated as " FAME ". 
 " dry cell wt " is abbreviated as " DCW ". 
 As used herein, term " invention " or " the present invention " are not intended to restriction but are usually applicable to any invention in claim or as herein described. 
 Term " peroxysome " refers to be prevalent in the organoid in all eukaryotic cells.They have independent lipid bilayer, and their content and cytosol are separated by this film, and comprise the required membranin of multiple hereinafter described function.Peroxysome is via " shuttle (extendedshuttlemechanism) of expansion " selectivity input albumen.More particularly, there are at least 32 known peroxidase body proteins (also referred to as peroxin), their participate in the process being inputted albumen by ATP hydrolysis through peroxisomal membrane.Some peroxidase body proteins comprise specific protein white signal at its N-end or C-end, that is, peroxysome target signal or " PTS ", and their pilot proteins pass through peroxisomal membrane.Once cell protein enters peroxysome, they are degraded by certain methods usually.Such as, peroxysome comprises oxydase, such as catalase, D-AAO and urico-oxidase, and these enzymes can be degraded the material poisonous to cell.Alternatively, peroxysome degraded fatty acid molecule is to generate acetyl-CoA free molecule, and they are fed back in cytosol, and this process is called β-oxidation. 
 Term " peroxysome biosynthesizing factor protein ", " peroxidase body protein " and " Pex albumen " are interchangeable, and reference and peroxysome is biosynthetic and/or participate in by ATP hydrolysis make cell protein pass the albumen of the process of peroxisomal membrane.The acronym of gene of these albumen any of encoding is " Pex genes ".The naming system of Pex gene is described in the people such as Distel, J.CellBiol., 135:1-3 (1996).In multiple eukaryote, at least 32 different Pex genes have been identified so far.From to having isolated multiple Pex gene the analysis of mutant, described mutant display has abnormal peroxysome function or structure.According to Kiel, J.A.K.W. document (the Traffic of people is waited, 7:1291-1303 (2006)), wherein the genome sequence in 17 different fungi strains is carried out to the bioinformatics analysis (silicoanalysis) of computer simulation, identify following Pex albumen: Pex1p, Pex2p, Pex3p, Pex3Bp, Pex4p, Pex5p, Pex5Bp, Pex5Cp, Pex5/20p, Pex6p, Pex7p, Pex8p, Pex10p, Pex12p, Pex13p, Pex14p, Pex15p, Pex16p, Pex17p, Pex14/17p, Pex18p, Pex19p, Pex20p, Pex21p, Pex21Bp, Pex22p, Pex22p sample and Pex26p.Therefore, each in these albumen is called " Pex albumen ", " peroxidase body protein " or " peroxysome biosynthesizing factor protein " herein, and each albumen is encoded by least one " Pex gene ". 
 At one group of amino acid that specific location is conservative in the aligned sequences of protein relevant in term " conserved domain " or " motif " fingering.Although can change at the amino acid of other position between homologous protein, being indicated as at the amino acid of specific position high conservative is essential amino acid structure, stability or activity concerning protein.Because they are identified by their high conservatives in the aligned sequences of protein homologs family, thus they can be used as protein that identification tag or " signature " determine to have new mensuration sequence whether belong to before the protein families of qualification.With reference to this paper relevant portion, Pex2p, Pex10p and Pex12p have a motif being rich in halfcystine at their C-terminal, and this motif known is C

         4 ring-type zinc-finger motif.This motif is that their activity is necessary, relates to albumen and stops and transfer to (Kiel, J.A.K.W., wait people, Traffic, 7:1291-1303 (2006)) in peroxysome.

 Term " lipid " refers to any fat-soluble (that is, lipophilic), naturally occurring molecule.Lipid is different groups of the compound with multiple critical biological function, the intermediate of the structural constituent of described function such as cytolemma, energy storage source and signal pathway.Lipid extensively can be defined as hydrophobicity or amphipathic small molecules, they completely or partially originate from ketoacyl or isoprene group.Table 2 shows the summary to lipid, and it is based on LipidMetabolitesandPathwaysStrategy (LIPIDMAPS) categorizing system (NationalInstituteofGeneralMedicalSciences, Bethesda, MD).

 lipid classification is summarized 
 
 
 
 
 All esterified fatty acids of " total lipid fraction " phalangeal cell of term cell herein.Separable different subfractions in total lipid fraction, comprise triacylglycerol [" oil "] fraction, phosphatidylcholine fraction and phosphatidylethanolamine fraction, but this do not comprise all subfractions. 
 " liposome " refers to by individual layer phosphatide and usually by lipid droplet that specific proteins combines.These organoids are sites of most of biology transport/storage neutral lipid.Think that liposome derives from the microcell of the endoplasmic reticulum comprising TAG biosynthetic enzyme.Their synthesis and size are subject to the control of specific protein components. 
 " neutral lipid " refers to the lipid in those cells being generally present in liposome with stored fat and oil form, and their title is that described lipid is without charged group because under cellular pH.They are generally completely nonpolar, to water without avidity.Neutral lipid refers generally to the monoglyceride of lipid acid, diester and/or three esters, is also called monoacylglycerol, DG or triacylglycerol, or is referred to as acylglycerol.In order to discharge free fatty acids from acylglycerol, hydrolysis reaction must be there is. 
 Term " triacylglycerol " [" TAG "] and " oil " are interchangeable, and they refer to by three of acylated glycerol molecule neutral lipids that fatty acyl residue forms.TAG can comprise long-chain PUFA, and shorter saturated with undersaturated lipid acid and the saturated fatty acid compared with long-chain.The TAG fraction of cell is also referred to as " oily fraction ", and " biosynthesizing of oil " refers generally to synthesize TAG in cell.Oil or TAG fraction are the subfractions of total lipid fraction, although it is also the major portion forming total lipid content, the per-cent that total lipid content accounts for dry cell wt [vide infra] with the total fatty acids weight in oil-containing biomass cells represents.Lipid acid composition in oil [" TAG "] fraction is generally similar with the lipid acid composition of total lipid fraction.Therefore, the raising of the PUFA concentration in total lipid fraction or reduction will corresponding to the rising of the PUFA concentration in oil [" TAG "] fraction or reductions, and vice versa. 
 Term " total fatty acids " [" TFA "] refers to the total amount of all cells lipid acid herein, described lipid acid changes into fatty acid methyl ester [" FAME "] by alkali ester exchange method (methods known in the art) is derived in given example, and such as it can be total lipid fraction or oily fraction.Therefore; total fatty acids comprises the lipid acid from neutral and polar lipid fraction; comprise phosphatidylcholine fraction, phosphatidylethanolamine fraction (phosphatidyletanolaminefraction) and DG, monoacylglycerol and triacylglycerol [" TAG or oil "] fraction, but do not comprise free fatty acids. 
 " total lipid content " of term cell is measuring of TFA, represents with the form of dry cell wt [" DCW "] per-cent.Therefore, total lipid content [" TFA%DCW "] is equal to the total fatty acids milligram number of such as every 100 milligrams of DCW. 
 Fatty acid concentration is generally expressed as the weight percent [" %TFA "] of TFA herein, the given lipid acid milligram number of such as every 100 milligrams of TFA.Unless separately illustrated in this paper disclosure, given lipid acid is equal to the fatty acid concentration (%EPA of such as TL is equal to EPA%TFA) represented with %TFA relative to the per-cent of TL. 
 In some cases, per-cent [" the %DCW "] form that given lipid acid in cell can be used to account for dry cell wt expresses the content of given lipid acid.Therefore such as timnodonic acid %DCW will measure according to following formula: (timnodonic acid %TFA) * (TFA%DCW)]/100. 
 Term " lipid profile " and " lipid composition " are interchangeable, and refer to the amount of the single lipid acid comprised in specific lipid fraction (such as in total lipid fraction or oil [" TAG "] fraction), wherein said amount TFA percents represents.The total amount of each single lipid acid existed in mixture should be 100. 
 As used herein, term " is multiplied " and refers to count by being multiplied by certain the increase obtained.Such as, by being multiplied by the quantity, amount, concentration, weight percent etc. of 1.3, the increase of 1.3 times is provided.

 Term " PUFA biosynthetic pathway " refers to metabolic process oleate conversion being become ω-6 lipid acid of such as LA, EDA, GLA, DGLA, ARA, DRA, DTA and DPAn-6 and so on and the omega-fatty acid of such as ALA, STA, ETrA, ETA, EPA, DPA and DHA and so on.This process is described in detail in document.See such as Int ' .App.Pub.No.WO2006/052870.In brief, this process relates to and extends carbochain by adding carbon atom and make molecule desaturation by adding double bond, and this is undertaken by being present in a series of specificity desaturase in endoplasmic reticulum and extending enzyme (being called " PUFA biosynthetic pathway enzyme ").More particularly, " PUFA biosynthetic pathway enzyme " refers to the following any enzyme relevant to PUFA biosynthesizing (and encode their gene), and described enzyme comprises: Δ 4 desaturase, Δ 5 desaturase, Δ 6 desaturase, Δ 12 desaturase, Δ 15 desaturase, Δ 17 desaturase, Δ 9 desaturase, Δ 8 desaturase, Δ 9 extend enzyme, C

 Term " Δ 6 desaturases/Δ 6 extends enzymatic pathway " refers to that minimum level comprises the PUFA biosynthetic pathway of at least one Δ 6 desaturase and at least one C18/20 extension enzyme, thus make respectively from LA and ALA, biosynthesizing DGLA and/or ETA to be carried out using GLA and/or STA as lipid acid intermediate product.By other desaturase and the expression extending enzyme, ARA, EPA, DPA and DHA can also be synthesized.

 Term " desaturase " refers to can by removing hydrogen atom from adjoining carbons and thus importing double bond to make a return journey the polypeptide of the adjoining carbons in saturated fatty acid between carbon atom.Desaturation creates lipid acid or concerned precursor.Although use the ω-system that refers to refer to specific lipid acid in whole specification sheets, Δ-system is used to represent that the activity of desaturase is more convenient from the carboxyl terminal counting of substrate.Special concern herein: 1) Δ 5 desaturase, its catalyze fatty acid substrate DGLA changes into ARA and/or catalyze fatty acid substrate ETA changes into EPA; 3) Δ 6 desaturase, its catalyze fatty acid substrate LA changes into GLA and/or catalyze fatty acid substrate A LA changes into STA; 4) Δ 12 desaturase, its catalytic substrate lipid acid oleic acid changes into LA; 5) Δ 15 desaturase, its catalyze fatty acid substrate LA changes into ALA and/or catalyze fatty acid substrate GLA changes into STA; 6) Δ 4 desaturase, its catalytic substrate lipid acid DPA changes into DHA and/or catalytic substrate lipid acid DTA changes into DPAn-6; 7) Δ 8 desaturase, its catalytic substrate lipid acid EDA changes into DGLA and/or catalytic substrate lipid acid ETrA changes into ETA; With, 8) Δ 9 desaturase, its catalytic substrate lipid acid palmitinic acid changes into Zoomeric acid (16:1) and/or catalytic substrate lipid acid stearic acid changes into oleic acid.Based on Δ 15 and Δ 17 desaturase, ω-6 convert fatty acids is become the ability (as respectively LA changed into ALA and ARA being changed into EPA) of their ω-3 counterpart, also they are called " ω-3 desaturase ", " W-3 desaturase " and/or " ω-3 desaturase " once in a while.It is desirable that by transforming suitable host with the gene of fatty acid desaturase and measuring its effect to this host's fatty acid distribution, thus empirically measure the specificity of special fatty acid desaturase.

 " Codon degeneracy " refers to the character of the genetic code changed when allowing nucleotides sequence to be listed in the aminoacid sequence not affecting coded polypeptide.Technician understands " codon preference " that concrete host cell shows when using nucleotide codon to determine given amino acid very much.Therefore, when synthetic gene is in order to improve the expression in host cell, ites is desirable to design gene, make its codon usage frequency close to the preferred codon usage frequency of this host cell.

 " gene " refers to the nucleic acid fragment of expressing specific protein, and can refer to that independent coding region maybe can comprise the regulating and controlling sequence before being positioned at encoding sequence (5 ' non-coding region) and regulating and controlling sequence (3 ' non-coding region) afterwards." natural gene " refers to the naturally occurring gene with its oneself regulating and controlling sequence." mosaic gene " refers to it is not any gene of natural gene, is not the regulating and controlling sequence and encoding sequence existed together under being included in its natural environment.Therefore, mosaic gene can comprise the regulating and controlling sequence and encoding sequence that come from different sources, or comprises and come from same source but to be different from the regulating and controlling sequence and encoding sequence that naturally occurring mode arranges." endogenous gene " refers to the natural gene being positioned at its natural place of biological genome." external " gene refers to the gene imported to by transgenosis in host living beings.Alien gene can comprise the natural gene of the natural gene be inserted in non-native organism, the new location imported in natural host, or mosaic gene." transgenosis " is by the gene in method for transformation quiding gene group." codon optimized gene " is that its codon usage frequency is through the gene of design in order to imitate the preferred codon usage frequency of host cell. 
 " encoding sequence " refers to the DNA sequence dna of encoding particular amino acid sequence." suitable regulating and controlling sequence " refers to be positioned at the upstream (5 ' non-coding sequence) of encoding sequence, the middle or nucleotide sequence of downstream (3 ' non-coding sequence), and it can affect the transcribing of related coding sequences, RNA processing or stability or translation.Regulating and controlling sequence can comprise promotor, enhanser, son of mourning in silence, 5 ' untranslated leader (sequence such as between transcription initiation site and translation setting up password), intron, polyadenylation recognition sequence, RNA Processing position, effector binding site and stem-ring structure. 
 " promotor " refers to can control coding sequence or the functional r NA DNA sequence dna of expressing.In general, encoding sequence is positioned at 3 ' end of promoter sequence.Promotor wholely can come from natural gene, or is made up of the different elements coming from different naturally occurring promotors, or even comprises the DNA fragmentation of synthesis.Those skilled in the art should be appreciated that different promotors can in different tissues or cell type, or in the different etap, or respond different envrionment conditionss or physiological condition and the expression of guiding gene.The promotor causing gene to be expressed in most cell types within the most of the time is commonly referred to " constitutive promoter ".Also be further appreciated that due in most of the cases regulating and controlling sequence really trimming circle determine not yet completely, therefore the DNA fragmentation of different lengths may have identical promoter activity. 
 Term " 3 ' non-coding sequence " and " transcription terminator " refer to the DNA sequence dna being positioned at encoding sequence downstream.This comprises polyadenylation recognition sequence and other sequence of the adjustment signal that can affect mRNA processing or genetic expression of encoding.Polyadenylation signal is characterised in that usually affects the 3 ' end that polyadenylic acid sheet adds mRNA precursor to.3rd ' district can affect the transcribing of related coding sequences, RNA processing or stability or translation. 
 " rna transcription thing " refers to transcribe produced product by RNA polymerase catalytic dna sequence.When rna transcription thing is the copy of the complete complementary of DNA sequence dna, it is called as primary transcript, or it can be derived from primary transcript the RNA sequence of transcribing post-treatment and be referred to as mature rna." messenger RNA(mRNA) " or " mRNA " refers to intronless and can be become the RNA of protein by cell translation." eDNA " refers to mRNA complementation and comes from the double-stranded DNA of mRNA.RNA refers to comprise mRNA and the rna transcription thing that thus can be become protein by cell translation " to have justice "." sense-rna " refers to and all or part of target primary transcript or mRNA complementation, and stops rna transcription thing (United States Patent (USP) 5,107,065 of expression of target gene; The open WO99/28508 of international application).Sense-rna can with any part of specific gene transcript, namely 5 ' non-coding sequence, 3 ' non-coding sequence or encoding sequence are complementary." functional r NA " refer to sense-rna, ribozyme rna or other be not translated but cell processes had to the RNA of influence. 
 Term " is operably connected " association of the nucleotide sequence referred on single core acid fragment, makes the function of one of them nucleotide sequence be subject to the impact of another nucleotide sequence.Such as, when promotor can affect the expression of encoding sequence, it is operably connected encoding sequence.That is, encoding sequence be in promotor transcribe control under.Encoding sequence can may be operably coupled to regulating and controlling sequence with the orientation of sense or antisense. 
 As used herein, what term " expression " referred to come from nucleic acid fragment has transcribing and stablely gathering of adopted RNA (mRNA) or sense-rna.Express and mRNA also can be referred to translate into polypeptide. 
 " maturation " albumen refers to the polypeptide through post translational processing, has namely eliminated and has been present in any propetide in initial translation product or the former polypeptide of peptide." precursor " protein refers to the primary translation product of mRNA, i.e. propetide and peptide is former still exists.Propetide and peptide is former can be but be not limited to intracellular localization signals. 
 " conversion " refers to nucleic acid molecule to be transferred in host living beings, causes genetic stability in heredity.Such as, nucleic acid molecule can be the plasmid of self-replicating, or it can be integrated in the genome of host living beings.Host living beings containing transformed nucleic acid fragments is called as " transgenosis " or " restructuring " or " conversion " organism. 
 " stable conversion " refers to be transferred to by nucleic acid fragment in the genome (comprising Matrix attachment region and organelle gene group) of host living beings, causes genetic stability in heredity.On the contrary, " instantaneous conversion " refers to nucleic acid fragment to be transferred in the core of host living beings or comprises in the organoid of DNA, causes genetic expression and unconformability or unstable heredity.Host living beings containing transformed nucleic acid fragments is called as " transgenosis " organism. 
 Term " plasmid " and " carrier " refer to usually carry the extra-chromosomal element of the gene not belonging to cell centre metabolism part, and are usually the forms of circular double stranded DNA fragment.This class component can be the nucleotide sequence (linear or ring-type) being derived from the autonomously replicating sequence in any source, genome integration sequence, phage or strand or double-stranded DNA or RNA, wherein multiple nucleotide sequence has connected or has been reassembled as a kind of unique design body, and expression cassette can be introduced in cell by this unique design body. 
 Term " expression cassette " refers to the DNA fragmentation comprising following encoding sequence: needed for the encoding sequence of selected gene and selected gene product expression be positioned at encoding sequence before the regulating and controlling sequence of (5 ' non-coding sequence) and (3 ' non-coding sequence) afterwards.Therefore, expression cassette is usually by following Sequence composition: (1) promoter sequence; 2) encoding sequence, that is, open reading frame [" ORF "] and, 3) 3 ' untranslated region, that is, in eukaryotic cell, usually comprise the terminator of polyadenylation site.Expression cassette is contained in carrier usually to be conducive to clone and to transform.Different expression cassette can be transformed in the different organisms comprising bacterium, yeast, plant and mammalian cell, as long as correct regulating and controlling sequence can be used for often kind of host.

 summary: the biosynthesizing of lipid acid and triacylglycerol 
 
 Usually, the accumulation of lipid in oil-containing microorganism responds total carbon-nitrogen ratio of being present in growth medium and triggers.This process (causing in oil-containing microorganism the de novo synthesis of free palmitinic acid (16:0)) at United States Patent (USP) 7,238, have a detailed description in 482.Palmitinic acid is the precursor of the saturated and unsaturated fatty acid derivative of long-chain, and these derivative of fatty acid form (Fig. 1) by the effect extending enzyme and desaturase. 
 TAG (primary storage unit of lipid acid) is formed by the series reaction relating to following reaction: acyl-CoA and the glycerol-3-phosphate of (1) a part generate Ultrapole L by acyltransferase esterification; (2) dimolecular acyl-CoAs generate 1 by acyltransferase esterification, 2-DG phosphoric acid (being commonly referred to phosphatidic acid); 3) phosphoric acid is removed to generate 1,2-DG [" DAG "] by phosphatidic acid phosphatase; With 4) add tri-fatty to form TAG by the effect of acyltransferase. 
 The lipid acid of wide spectrum can be introduced in TAG, comprises saturated with undersaturated lipid acid and the lipid acid of short chain and long-chain.Some limiting examples being introduced into the lipid acid of TAG by acyltransferase comprise: capric acid (10:0), lauric acid (12:0), tetradecanoic acid (14:0), palmitinic acid (16:0), Zoomeric acid (16:1), stearic acid (18:0), oleic acid (18:1), isooleic acid (18:1), LA (18:2), eleostearic acid (18:3), GLA (18:3), ALA (18:3), STA (18:4), eicosanoic acid (20:0), EDA (20:2), DGLA (20:3), ETrA (20:3), ARA (20:4), ETA (20:4), EPA (20:5), docosoic acid (22:0), DPA (22:5), DHA (22:6), lignoceric acid (24:0), Selacholeic acid (24:1), cerinic acid (26:0) and montanic acid (28:0) lipid acid.In method as herein described and host cell, expect " long-chain " PUFA to introduce in TAG most, wherein long-chain PUFA comprises any lipid acid deriving from 18:1 substrate, and described substrate has at least 18 carbon atoms, that is, C
         18 or it is longer.It also comprises hydroxylated fatty acid, epoxyfatty acid and conjugated linolic acid.
       
 Although most of PUFA mixes TAG with the form of neutral lipid and is stored in liposome, importantly recognize that in oil-containing biology, measure total PUFA should comprise the PUFA that those are arranged in phosphatidylcholine fraction, phosphatidylethanolamine fraction and triacylglycerol (also referred to as TAG or oil) fraction. 
 
 the biosynthesizing of omega-3 fatty acid 
 
 Wherein oleate conversion become the metabolic process of ω-3/ ω-6 lipid acid comprise by add carbon atom make carbochain extend and make molecule desaturation by adding double bond.This needs to be present in a series of special desaturase in endoplasmic reticulum and extension enzyme.But, as see in FIG with as described below, usually there is multiple alternative route for generation of specific ω-3/ ω-6 lipid acid. 
 Specifically, Fig. 1 describes approach hereinafter described.All approach all need by Δ 12 desaturase, oleate conversion to be become linolic acid LA (first ω-6 lipid acid) at first.Then, utilize " Δ 6 desaturases/Δ 6 extends enzymatic pathway " and LA is formed long-chain omega-6 lipid acid as follows as substrate: 1) by Δ 6 desaturase, LA being changed into gamma-linolenic acid [" GLA "]; 2) C is passed through
         18/20 extend enzyme and GLA is changed into dihomo-gamma-linolenic acid [" DGLA "]; 3) by Δ 5 desaturase, DGLA is changed into arachidonic acid [" ARA "]; 4) C is passed through
         20/22 extend enzyme and ARA is changed into docosatetratenoic acid [" DTA "]; And, 5) by Δ 4 desaturase, DTA is changed into clupanodonic acid [" DPAn-6 "].
       
 Alternatively, " Δ 6 desaturases/Δ 6 extends enzymatic pathway " can use alpha-linolenic acid [" ALA "] to make substrate as follows and produce long-chain omega-fatty acid: LA is changed into ALA (first omega-fatty acid) by Δ 15 desaturase by (1); 2) by Δ 6 desaturase, ALA is changed into therapic acid [" STA "]; 3) C is passed through
         18/20 extend enzyme and STA is changed into eicosatetraenoic acid [" ETA "]; 4) by Δ 5 desaturase, ETA is changed into timnodonic acid [" EPA "]; 5) C is passed through
         20/22 extend enzyme and EPA is changed into clupanodonic acid [" DPA "]; And, 6) by Δ 4 desaturase, DPA is changed into docosahexenoic acid [" DHA "].Optionally, ω-6 lipid acid can change into omega-fatty acid; Such as, ETA and EPA is generated from DGLA and ARA respectively by Δ 17 desaturase activity.
       
 The alternative route of ω-3/ ω-6 fatty acid biological synthesis utilizes Δ 9 to extend enzyme and Δ 8 desaturase, that is, " Δ 9 extends enzyme/Δ 8 desaturase approach ".More particularly, LA and ALA extends enzyme by Δ 9 and changes into EDA and ETrA respectively; Then EDA is changed into DGLA and/or ETrA is changed into ETA by Δ 8 desaturase.Form downstream PUFA as mentioned above subsequently. 
 Herein host living beings must be natural or have the ability of production PUFA via genetic engineering technique.Although multiple-microorganism can synthesize PUFA (comprising ω-3/ ω-6 lipid acid) in common cellular process, and some in them can carry out business cultivation, but these biological seldom produce or do not produce the oil-contg with expectation oil and for the composition in medicine, dietary substitute, dietetic food, nutritious supplementary, other foodstuff products, commercial grease chemical preparations or other end product.Therefore, more and more focus on that engineered microorganisms is with the ability of the lipid and oil of producing " design ", wherein fatty acid content and composition are specified in detail by genetically engineered.On this basis, expect that host may comprise the heterologous gene of encode functional PUFA biosynthetic pathway, but this is nonessential. 
 If the PUFA that the not natural production of host living beings is expected or the lipid profile with expectation, those skilled in the art are afamiliar with the necessary design of host living beings selected by one or more expression cassettes importings and technology that coding are used for the biosynthetic suitable enzymes of PUFA.Document is multiple instruction for technician provides, for this type of expression cassette is imported multiple host living beings.There is provided as follows by using some documents of host living beings Yarrowia lipolytica: United States Patent (USP) 7,238,482, international application published WO2006/033723, public announcement of a patent application US-2006-0094092, public announcement of a patent application US-2006-0115881-A1 and public announcement of a patent application US-2006-0110806-A1.Above-mentioned enumerate and non-exclusive therefore should not be construed as restrictive. 
 In brief, multiple ω-3/ ω-6PUFA product can be produced before they change into TAG, this specific gene depending on fatty acid substrate and be present in or be transformed into ω-3/ ω-6 fatty acid biosynthetic pathway in host cell.Similarly, expect that the production of fatty acid product may directly occur or indirectly occur.When without any intermediate steps or intermediate approach fatty acid substrate directly being changed into the fatty acid product of expectation, direct production occurs.When multiple genes of coding PUFA biosynthetic pathway can be combined uses, when series reaction is occurred with the PUFA producing expectation, indirectly produce generation.Specifically, can expect with comprising Δ 12 desaturase, Δ 6 desaturase, C
         18/20 the expression cassette extending enzyme, Δ 5 desaturase and Δ 17 desaturase transforms saccharomyces olei and produces EPA with surplus.See United States Patent (USP) 7,238,482 and international application published WO2006/052870.For well-known to those having ordinary skill in the art be other combination multiple of the gene of coding PUFA biosynthetic pathway enzyme can be used for expressing (see Fig. 1) in oil-containing biology.Be contained in the concrete gene embodied in box depend on host living beings, it PFUA distribution and/or desaturase/extensions enzyme distributes, the utilizability of substrate and the end product of expectation.
       
 Many candidate genes have required desaturase and/or elongase activity, and their can be identified according to disclose obtainable document, as GenBank, patent documentation and the experimental analysis carried out the biology with production PUFA ability.Available desaturase and extension enzyme sequence can be derived from any source, such as, are separated from natural origin as bacterium, algae, fungi, oomycetes, yeast, plant, animal etc., via semi-synthetic approach generation or de novo synthesis.After these candidate genes of qualification, consideration item when having the specific polypeptide of desaturase or elongase activity is selected to comprise: the 1) substrate specificity of polypeptide; 2) whether polypeptide or its assembly are rate-limiting enzyme; 3) whether desaturase or extension enzyme are that the PUFA that synthesis is expected is necessary; 4) cofactor needed for polypeptide; And/or 5) whether polypeptide modified after its formation, such as, modified by kinases or prenyltransferase. 
 The polypeptide of expressing preferably has the compatible parameter of the biochemical environment of the position with it in host cell.See United States Patent (USP) 7,238,482.It also can be useful for considering often kind of specific desaturase and/or extending the transformation efficiency of enzyme.More particularly, because substrate conversion seldom can be become product with the efficiency of 100% by often kind of enzyme, the mixture of the multiple PUFA that the final lipid profile of the unpurified oil produced in host cell is normally made up of ω-3/ ω-6 lipid acid expected and multiple upstream PUFA intermediate product.Therefore, when making the biosynthesizing optimization of lipid acid of expectation, the efficiency of conversion of often kind of enzyme is also the variable that will consider.

 Alternatively, disclosing obtainable Pex sequence or their motif can be hybridizing reagent for the identification of homologue.The essentially consist of nucleic acid hybridization assay comprises probe, suspects the sample and specific hybridizing method that contain goal gene or gene fragment.Probe normally with the single strand nucleotide sequence of nucleic acid array complementation to be detected.Probe and nucleotide sequence to be detected are interfertile.Although the length of probe can change between tens thousand of bases 5 bases, usual about 15 bases are suitable to the probe length of about 30 bases.Only need the part of probe molecule and nucleic acid array complementation to be detected.In addition, complete complementary is not needed between probe and target sequence.Hybridization can occur really between the molecule of not complete complementary, and result is that the base of certain ratio in hybridization region is not matched with suitable complementary base. 
 Hybridizing method is known.Usual probe and sample must mix under the condition allowing nucleic acid hybridization.This relates to makes probe and sample contacts when there is inorganic or organic salt under proper concn and temperature condition.Probe must contact the sufficiently long time with sample nucleic, and any possible hybridization between probe and sample nucleic all can be occurred.The concentration of the probe in mixture or target determines the time needed for hybridization generation.The concentration of probe or target is higher, and the required hybridization incubation time is shorter.Optionally, chaotropic agent (as chlorination guanidine, guanidine thiocyanate, Sodium Thiocyanate 99, tetrachloro lithium acetate, sodium perchlorate, tetrachloro rubidium acetate, potassiumiodide or trifluoroacetic acid caesium) can be added.If needed, methane amide can be added hybridization mixture, be generally 30-50% (v/v) [" by volume "]. 
 Multiple hybridization solution can be adopted.Usually, these hybridization solutions comprise about 20% to 60% volume, preferably the polar organic solvent of 30% volume.Common hybridization solution adopt about 30-50%v/v methane amide, about 0.15 to 1M sodium-chlor, about 0.05 to 0.1M damping fluid (as Trisodium Citrate, Tris-HCl, PIPES or HEPES (pH scope is about 6-9)), about 0.05 to 0.2% stain remover (as sodium lauryl sulphate) or EDTA, FICOLL (PharmaciaInc.) (about 300-500 kilodalton) of 0.5-20mM, polyvinylpyrrolidone (about 250-500 kilodalton) and serum albumin.General hybridization solution also comprises the nucleic acid DNA (as calf thymus or salmon sperm DNA or yeast rna) of the vector nucleic acid of about 0.1 to 5mg/mL un-marked, fragmentation, and the glycine of optional about 0.5% to 2%wt/vol [" weightmeasurement ratio "].Other additive can be comprised, such as, comprise the volume-exclusion agent of polar water soluble or inflatable reagent (as polyoxyethylene glycol), anionic polymer (as polyacrylic ester or polymethacrylate) and anionic saccharidic polymers (as T 500). 
 Nucleic acid hybridization is applicable to many measure form.One of most suitable form is sandwich assay formats.Sandwich assay is particularly useful for hybridizing under non denatured condition.The main component of sandwich-type assays is solid support.Solid support has absorption or the fixed nucleic acid probe that is covalently attached on it, this probe un-marked and complementary with a part for sequence.

 Be preferably to the resistance of kantlex, Totomycin and aminoglycoside G418 for the system of selection of Yarrowia lipolytica and lacking the ability that the substratum of uridylic, leucine, Methionin, tryptophane or Histidine grows.5-fluororotic acid [5 FU 5 fluorouracil-6-carboxylic acid monohydrate or " 5-FOA "] also can be used for selecting yeast Ura-mutant.The yeast cell of this compound to the functional URA3 gene with coding vitamin B13 glycosides 5 '-monophosphate decarboxylase [OMP decarboxylase] is toxic; Therefore, based on this toxicity, 5-FOA is particularly useful for selecting and qualification Ura-mutant yeast bacterial strain (Bartel, P.L. and Fields, S., Yeast2-HybridSystem, OxfordUniversity:NewYork, 7th volume, 109-147 page, 1997; Also see the open WO2006/052870 of international application, for the application of 5-FOA in Ye Shi yeast belong). 
 Alternative method for preferential selection for Ye Shi yeast belong depend on for Yarrowia lipolytica based on sulfonylurea (chlorimuronethyl; E.I.duPontdeNemours & Co., Inc., Wilmington, DE) the dominant non-antibiotic marker of resistance.More particularly, this marker gene has natural acetohydroxy acid synthase (" AHAS " or the acetolactate synthase that single amino acids changes (i.e. W497L); Thus impart sulfonylurea herbicide resistance (international application published WO2006/052870) E.C.4.1.3.18).AHAS is for the conventional enzyme of first in the approach of biosynthesizing branched-chain amino acid (i.e. α-amino-isovaleric acid, leucine, Isoleucine), and it is the target of sulfonylurea and imidazolidinone weedicide. 
 
 for the fermentation process that polyunsaturated fatty acid is produced

 the purifying of PUFA oil and process 
 
 The lipid acid comprising PUFA can free fatty acids or esterified form such as acylglycerol, phosphatide, thioester or glycolipid form be present in host living beings.These lipid acid extract from host cell by multiple method well known in the art.One section of summary about the extractive technique of yeast lipid, mass analysis and acceptable standard is the summary of Z.Jacobs (CriticalReviewsinBiotechnology, 12 (5/6): 463-491 (1992)).The summary of associated downstream processing also can be provided by A.Singh and O.Ward (Adv.Appl.Microbiol., 45:271-312 (1997)). 
 In general, means for purification of fatty acid (comprising PUFA) can comprise uses organic solvent extraction (such as, United States Patent (USP) 6,797,303 and United States Patent (USP) 5,648,564), supersound process, supercritical fluid extraction (as used carbonic acid gas), saponification and physical means (such as extruding) or their combination.See United States Patent (USP) 7,238,482.

 These compositions can give healthy and helpful effect by joining in dietetic food (comprising medical nutritious material, dietary supplement, infant formula and medicine).Technician will know and is added in food, feed, dietary supplement, nutritive substance, medicine and other ingestible product to give the amount of the oil of healthy and helpful effect.Art describes the healthy and helpful effect that these oil of picked-up obtain, it is known to the skilled and the research continued.Amount as referred to herein is " effectively " amount, except the reason of other side, it depend on the character comprising the product of these oil of absorption and they be intended to the illness for the treatment of.

         20 the amount (representing with dry cell wt percents) of PUFA or all PUFA improves (parent strain relative to natural Pex albumen is not destroyed).In other cases, in total lipid fraction and oily fraction, there is the C of the reduction represented with dry cell wt percents
         20 pUFA or all PUFA (parent strain relative to natural Pex albumen is not destroyed).Also observe the similar results relative to total lipid content (TFA%DCW), the effect that therefore Pex destroys may cause total lipid content to improve or reduce.
       
 Although every content of above-outlined is all concerned, what be particularly useful is check that Pex destroys the effect to the ratio that the PUFA expected measures relative to total PUFA, carries out through engineering approaches to produce the PUFA expected to biology. 
 Such as, in the bacterial strain Y4128 comprising Pex10 destruction, the PUFA (%TFA) of 54% is EPA, described destruction causes last 32 amino acid clipping C-terminal, but in parent strain Y4086, only have the PUFA of 16.3% (%TFA) to be EPA.Therefore, described destruction causes the PUFA (%TFA) expected to measure raising 3.3 times (embodiment 3,4).In a similar situation, in bacterial strain Y4036 (Δ Pex16), the PUFA (%TFA) of 62.8% is DGLA, but in Y4036-, only have the PUFA of 38.1% (%TFA) to be DGLA, improve 1.65 times (embodiments 9).And in bacterial strain Y4036 (Δ Pex3), the PUFA (%TFA) of 67.7% is DGLA, but only has the PUFA of 33.3% (%TFA) to be DGLA in Y4036-, improve 2.0 times (embodiments 12).These results confirm this hypothesis: Pex destroys and causes the amount (%TFA) of the PUFA of the expectation in total lipid fraction and oily fraction optionally to improve, and described PUFA is produced by engineered biological. 
 When checking the effect that Pex destroys the ratio that C20PUFA measures relative to total PUFA, observe lower selectivity.Such as, in the bacterial strain Y4128 comprising Pex10 destruction, the PUFA (%TFA) of 73% is C20PUFA, but in bacterial strain Y4086, only has the PUFA of 42% (%TFA) to be C20PUFA.Therefore, destruction causes the C20PUFA gathered in total lipid fraction and oily fraction to improve 1.7 times (embodiments 3,4) relative to the amount of total PUFA.In a similar situation, in bacterial strain Y4036 (Δ Pex16), the PUFA (%TFA) of 71% is C20PUFA, but in Y4036-, only have the PUFA of 54.8% (%TFA) to be C20PUFA, improve 1.3 times (embodiments 9).And the PUFA (%TFA) of 82.4% is C20PUFA in bacterial strain Y4036 (Δ Pex3), but in Y4036-, only have the PUFA of 47.4% (%TFA) to be C20PUFA, improve 1.7 times (embodiments 12).

 the conversion of Yarrowia lipolytica and cultivation 
 
 Yarrowia lipolytica strain ATCC#20362 purchased from American Type Tissue Collection (Rockville, MD).Cultivate at 28-30 DEG C in the several mediums of Yarrowia lipolytica strain formula shown in normally below basis.According to standard method, prepare agar plate as desired, by being added in often kind of liquid nutrient medium by 20g/L agar. 
   yPD Agar substratum (often liter) : 10g yeast extract [Difco], 20g bactopeptone [Difco] and 20g glucose.
       
   minimum medium (MM) (often liter) : 20g glucose, 1.7g are without amino acid yeast nitrogen, 1.0g proline(Pro), and pH6.1 (not needing to regulate).
       
   minimum medium+uridylic (MM+ uridylic or MMU) (often liter) : as above prepare MM substratum and add 0.1g uridylic and 0.1g uridine.
       
   minimum medium+uridylic+sulfonylurea (MMU+SU) (often liter) : as above prepare MMU substratum and add 280mg sulfonylurea.
       
   minimum medium+leucine+Methionin (MMLeuLys) (often liter) : as above prepare MM substratum and add 0.1g leucine and 0.1g Methionin.
       
   minimum medium+5-fluororotic acid (MM+5-FOA) (often liter) : 20a glucose, 6.7g yeast nitrogen, 75mg uridylic, 75mg uridine, and based on the FOA activity test (can change because of every batch of material that supplier provides) to a series of concentration from 100mg/L to 1000mg/L, select appropriate FOA (ZymoResearchCorp., Orange, CA).

 The conversion of Yarrowia lipolytica completes according to the method for the people such as Chen, D.C. (Appl.MicrobiolBiotechnol., 48 (2): 232-235 (1997)), unless otherwise indicated.In brief, Ye Shi yeast is scoring on YPD flat board, and at 30 DEG C, grows about 18 hours.From flat board wipe off several large circular rector cell and be resuspended to containing below composition lmL transfer buffer in: 2.25mL50%PEG, molecular-weight average is 3350; 0.125mL2M Lithium Acetate, pH6.0; And 0.125mL2MDTT.Then, linearizing for about 500ng plasmid DNA is hatched in the cell of 100 μ L resuspensions, and it is maintained 1 hour at 39 DEG C, carried out vortex mixed at interval of 15 minutes.Cell to be layered on Selective agar medium flat board and to maintain 2 to 3 days at 30 DEG C. 
 
 the fatty acid analysis of Yarrowia lipolytica 
 
 In order to carry out fatty acid analysis, cell is also extracted lipid by collected by centrifugation as described in Bligh, E.G. & Dyer, W.J. (Can.J.Biochem.Physiol., 37:911-917 (1959)).By lipid-soluble extract and sodium methylate are carried out transesterification reaction and prepare fatty acid methyl ester [" FAME " (Roughan, and NishidaI. G., ArchBiochemBiophys., 276 (1): 38-46 (1990)) and subsequently it is analyzed with the Hewlett-Packard6890 gas chromatograph (GC) being furnished with 30m × 0.25mm (internal diameter) HP-INNOWAX (Hewlett-Packard) post.Furnace temperature is raised to 185 DEG C with 3.5 DEG C/min from 170 DEG C (keeping 25 minutes). 
 In order to carry out direct base-catalyzed transesterification reaction, results Ye Shi yeast culture (3mL), wash once in distilled water, and in Speed-Vac dry 5-10 minute under vacuo.Sodium methylate (100 μ L, concentration is 1%) is added in sample, then by sample vortex oscillation 20 minutes.After adding 3 1M sodium-chlor and 400 μ L hexanes, vortex centrifugal sample.Shift out upper strata and GC described above analyzes.
